# Pick a source for session. 
galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
# galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
# pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

#Focus(source)

#ResetConfig()

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to X-band (Rcvr8_10). Click yes when Xband is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "Rcvr8_10"})
SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":9000})

AutoPeakFocus(source,configure=True) 

#Break("enter pointing offsets")

#Focus(source) 

#Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

#ResetConfig()

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source

# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1

# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4

# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
# galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

print "Integration time per row (s): ", mymap['scanDuration']

           Offset("J2000", mymap['mapHeight']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['scanLength']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", mymap['step']/3600., 0.0, cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
# oofSrc='0319+4130'
oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
# fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1
fluxSrc = '2253+1608'

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
# oofSrc='0319+4130'
oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1
#fluxSrc = '2253+1608'

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
# galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1
#fluxSrc = '2253+1608'

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
# pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat")

print "Mapping galaxy: ", galaxyName
print "Integration time per row (s): ", mymap['scanDuration']
print "Offset between map rows (arcsec): ", mymap['step']
print "Length of scan (arcmin): ", mymap['scanLength']
print "Height of map (arcmin): ",  mymap['mapHeight']

Configure(argus_config)
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(galaxyName)
Balance()

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

RALongMap( galaxyName,
           Offset("J2000", mymap['scanLength']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0,  mymap['mapHeight']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['step']/3600., cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
# galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
# galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source
galaxyName = "NGC2623" #test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1
#fluxSrc = '2253+1608'

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
# pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
# pointSrc="0027+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

           Offset("J2000", mymap['mapHeight']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['scanLength']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", mymap['step']/3600., 0.0, cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

# Pick a source for session. 
# galaxyName = "NGC0169" # source 1 around 20:30
# galaxyName = "NGC0932" # source 2 around 22:30
# galaxyName = "UGC02239" # source 3 around 00:30 only RAmap
# galaxyName = "UGC04262" # source 4 around 01:30
# galaxyName = "NGC2449" # source 5 around 03:30
# galaxyName = "UGC04258" # source 6 around 05:30
galaxyName = "UGC05187" # extra source for end around 06:30
# galaxyName = "IC1683" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2253" # test source
# galaxyName = "NGC2623" #test source

# AutoOOF source
oofSrc='0319+4130'
# oofSrc='2253+1608' # for OOF around 01:30

# Flux scalibration source 
fluxSrc = '0319+4130' # good for source 1
#fluxSrc = '2253+1608'

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
# pointSrc="0042+2320" # good for source 1
# pointSrc="0237+2848" # good for source 2 and 3
# pointSrc="1153+8058" # good for source 4
# pointSrc="0741+3112" # good for source 5
# pointSrc="0813+4813" # good for source 6
pointSrc="0927+3902" # good for extra source

print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin
